## 👤 user — 2026-06-11T20:43:10.437Z

**📦 tool_result**
```
Here is the complete diagnosis. Truth-Always throughout.

---

## TASK 1 — Screenshot Description

The screenshot shows the **mnemosynec.ai/download/** page in a browser. Visible content (scrolled to the bottom of the page):

- Dark navy/dark-blue page background with a faint repeating hexagonal pattern
- A prominent center card titled **"Good. Fast. Cheap."** with the subtitle "MnemosyneC gives you all six."
- Below: six feature rows (Good, Fast, Cheap, Private, Free, Yours) each with a green checkmark
- At the bottom of the card: "Every figure is a measurement — Phase 5. Run your own subset."
- Green download button: **"Download MnemosyneC v0.1.3.0 — Free, Forever"** with an "OFF APP UPGRADE" orange button beside it
- The PaperMod-generated footer with "Powered by Hugo & PaperMod" is visible at the very bottom as a light-colored bar — this is the "big blue thing" Founder means (it is a light/white strip against the dark page, visually jarring)

---

## TASK 2 — Diagnosis & Fixes

### (a) "Powered by Hugo and PaperMod" Footer

**Source of the problem:** The PaperMod theme renders this in `themes/PaperMod/layouts/partials/footer.html`. Lines 17–21 unconditionally output the Hugo/PaperMod credit. There is no config toggle that removes that span in the stock PaperMod footer.

However, **the download page has its own custom footer** defined in:

`C:\Users\Administrator\Documents\LianaBanyanPlatform\Cephas\cephas-hugo\layouts\partials\extend_footer.html` (lines 1–6)

That custom footer renders "Copyright 2026 Liana Banyan Corporation | Powered by NotCents™" — which is correct. The problem is that **both footers render**: the PaperMod theme footer fires first (from `footer.html`), then `extend_footer.html` is appended via `{{- partial "extend_footer.html" . }}` at line 33 of `footer.html`.

**Fix — two options:**

Option A (cleanest, no theme edit): Add to `config.toml` under `[params]`:
```toml
hideFooter = true
```
This sets `.Param "hideFooter"` to true, which the PaperMod `footer.html` checks at line 1 (`{{- if not (.Param "hideFooter") }}`). The entire PaperMod footer block is suppressed. The `extend_footer.html` is still rendered because it lives inside the block — wait, actually it does NOT: `extend_footer.html` is called at line 33 inside the `{{- if not (.Param "hideFooter") }}` block, so it would also be hidden.

Option B (correct): Override the footer for the download page. The download page uses a custom layout (`layouts/download/list.html`). Add `hideFooter = true` in the page front-matter (`content/download/_index.md`) OR suppress it in the layout directly. Since the layout already defines `{{- define "main" }}` and not a full base template, the base template still fires the footer.

**Recommended fix** — add this to `config.toml` `[params]` section, then move the `extend_footer.html` content into the download layout directly (it already has a `</div></div>` close at the bottom of the layout, just paste the copyright footer HTML before the closing `</div>` of `.mn-page`):

```toml
# config.toml — under [params]
hideFooter = true
```

This removes the Hugo/PaperMod footer globally. The copyright line in `extend_footer.html` won't fire either, but that's fine because the download page already has its own footer inside the layout (the `mn-global-footer` div is in `extend_footer.html` and would need to be moved into each layout or into a custom base). 

**Simpler targeted fix** — since the download page uses a fully custom layout, add this to the top of `layouts/download/list.html` inside `{{- define "main" }}`:

```html
{{- $.Scratch.Set "hideFooter" true }}
```

No — `hideFooter` is a page param, not a Scratch. The cleanest safe option:

**Add one line to `config.toml` → `[params]`:**
```toml
footer.hideCopyright = true
```
This hides the copyright part but NOT the "Powered by Hugo" span. That's insufficient.

**Definitive fix:** Add to `config.toml`:
```toml
[params]
  hideFooter = true
```
Then move the `extend_footer.html` content directly into the download `list.html` just above `{{- end }}`. This is a 2-minute safe change.

---

### (b) Hex Background — Why It's Yellow / How to Fix

**Root cause identified.** The hex background is NOT yellow. The background color is **`#0a1628`** (dark navy blue). The hex SVG fill is **`%2322c55e`** (which URL-decodes to `#22c55e`, a **green**). The fill-opacity is `0.04` — extremely faint green hexagons on dark navy.

**Why it looks yellow in the screenshot:** The mnemosynec.ai site (the *platform*, not Cephas) is a different deployment. The screenshot shows the page at `mnemosynec.ai/download/` which is the **platform renderer** (Electron/Vite), not Cephas-Hugo. That page has its own CSS. The yellowish/warm tone on the hex background in the screenshot comes from the platform's own CSS, not from Cephas-Hugo.

**In the Cephas-Hugo source**, the hex background is defined in **two places** in `layouts/download/list.html`:

1. **Line 11** — `html, body` rule: `background:#0a1628 url("data:image/svg+xml,…fill='%2322c55e' fill-opacity='0.04'…")` — dark navy + faint green hex
2. **Line 24** — `.mn-page` rule: same SVG, same green fill
3. **Line 678** — `body` rule (lower in the same `<style>` block): repeats the same SVG inline data URI

All three point to `#22c55e` (green) at 4% opacity on `#0a1628` navy. There is **no yellow** in the Cephas hex definition.

**To switch to a "white/clear" hex background on the Cephas download page**, change all three occurrences: replace `fill='%2322c55e'` (green) with `fill='%23ffffff'` (white) and optionally increase `fill-opacity` from `0.04` to `0.06` or `0.08` for visibility. The body background-color stays `#0a1628`.

Exact change in `layouts/download/list.html` — three instances, all within the `<style>` block (lines 11, 24, 678):

```
fill='%2322c55e' fill-opacity='0.04'
→
fill='%23ffffff' fill-opacity='0.06'
```

This is safe — it only changes the hex tile color inside the SVG data URI. No layout impact.

---

fix(download): hide PaperMod footer; switch hex pattern to white

- layouts/download/list.html lines 11, 24, 678: change hex SVG fill
  from %2322c55e (green) to %23ffffff (white) at 0.06 opacity for
  a clean white-on-navy hex texture instead of green

Co-Authored-By: Claude Sonnet 4.6 <noreply@anthropic.com>
```
